 4488  As noted earlier, cardiac myocytes are myogenic and require no external stimulus in order to\ncontract. A heart can be removed from an animal (isolating it from the nervous and endocrine\nsystems of coordination) and it will continue to contract for sometime.  4500  class Solution:\n    def maxSubArray(self, nums: List[int]) -> int:\n\t    """\n\t\ttc - O(n)\n\t\tsc - O(1), since python iterators use lazy evaluation\n\t\t"""\n        return max(itertools.accumulate(nums, lambda a, b: max(b, a+b)))\n\t\t\n\t\t#     [1,1,-3,4,0,1,-1,-2,4]  example\n\t\t#     [1,2,-1,4,4,5, 4, 2,6] -> after accumulate\n

  private List<T> adj[]; //Adjacency Lists\n \n    // Constructor\n    bfsOrder(int v)\n    {\n        V = v;\n        adj = new List[v];\n        for (int i=0; i<v; ++i)\n            adj[i] = new List();\n    }\n \n    // Function to add an edge into the bfsOrder\n    void addEdge(int v,int w)\n    {\n        adj[v].add(w);\n    }\n \n    // prints BFS traversal from a given source s\n    void BFS(int s)\n    {\n        // Mark all the vertices as not visited(By default\n        // set as false)\n        boolean visited[] = new boolean[V];\n \n        // Create a queue for BFS\n        List<Integer> queue = new List<Integer>();\n \n        // Mark the current node as visited and enqueue it\n        visited[s]=true;\n        queue.add(s);\n \n        while (queue.size() != 0)\n        {\n            // Dequeue a vertex from queue and print it\n            s = queue.poll();\n            System.out.print(s+" ");\n \n            // Get all adjacent vertices of the dequeued vertex s\n      {\n                int n = i.next();\n                if (!visited[n])\n                {\n                    visited[n] = true;\n                    queue.add(n);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n \n    // Driver method to\n    public static void main(String args[])\n    {\n        bfsOrder g = new bfsOrder(4);\n \n        g.addEdge(0, 1);\n        g.addEdge(0, 2);\n private BSTNode<E> root; // Root of the BST\n    private int occurs; // Number of nodes in the BST\n  \n    // constructor\n    BST() { root = null; occurs = 0; }\n  \n    // Reinitialize tree\n    public void clear() { root = null; occurs = 0; }\n  \n    // Insert a record into the tree.\n    // Records can be anything, but they must be Comparable\n    // e: The record to insert.\n    public        occurs--;\n      }\n      return temp;\n    }\n  \n    // Return the record with key value k, null if none exists\n    // key: The key value to find\n    public E find(E key) { return "([{}])" is properly well formed. \n\nimport java.util.*;\n \npublic class WellFormed {\n \n    // function to check if brackets are balanced\n    static boolean wellFormed(String s)\n    {\n        // Using ArrayDeque is faster than using Stack class\n        Deque<Character> stack\n            = new ArrayDeque<Character>();\n \n        // Traversing the expression\n        for (int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++)\n        {\n            char x = s.charAt(i);\n \n            if (x == '(' || x == '[' || x == '{')\n            {\n                // Push the element in the stack\n                stack.push(x);\n                continue;\n            }\n \n            // If current character is not opening\n            // bracket, then it must be closing. So stack\n            // cannot be empty at this point.\n            if (stack.isEmpty())\n                return false;\n            char check;\n            switch (x) {\n            case ')':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '{' || check == '[')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n \n            case '}':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '(' || check == '[')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n \n            case ']':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '(' || check == '{')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n \n        // Check Empty Stack\n        return (stack.isEmpty());\n    }\n \n    // Driver code\n    public static void main(String[] args)\n    {\n        String s = "([{}])";\n \n        // Function call\n        if (wellFormed(s))\n            System.out.println("Balanced ");\n        else\n            System.out.println("Not Balanced ");\n    }\n}Chris Samuel\n24141468\nHomework 6 Iterative Functions\n\n\n#### static <T> leftMost(BTNode<T> root): Returns \n### the        occurs--;\n      }\n      return temp;\n    }\n  \n    // Return the record with key value k, null if none exists\n    // key: The key value to find\n    public E find(E key) { return findhelp(root, key); }\n  \n    // Return the number of records in the dictionary\n    public int size() { return occurs; }\n\n    // static boolean wellFormed(String s): Tests if a given string of "([{}])" is properly well formed. \n\nimport java.util.*;\n \npublic class WellFormed {\n \n    // function to check if brackets are balanced\n    static boolean wellFormed(String s)\n    {\n        // Using ArrayDeque is faster than using Stack class\n        Deque<Character> stack\n            = new ArrayDeque<Character>();\n \n        // Traversing the expression\n        for (int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++)\n        {\n            char x = s.charAt(i);\n \n            if (x == '(' || x == '[' || x == '{')\n            {\n                // Push the element in the stack\n                stack.push(x);\n                continue;\n            }\n \n            // If current character is not opening\n            // bracket, then it must be closing. So stack\n            // cannot be empty at this point.\n            if (stack.isEmpty())\n                return false;\n            char check;\n            switch (x) {\n            case ')':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '{' || check == '[')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n \n            case '}':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '(' || check == '[')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n \n            case ']':\n                check = stack.pop();\n                if (check == '(' || check == '{')\n                    return false;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n \n        // Check Empty Stack\n        return (stack.isEmpty());\n    }\n \n    // Driver code\n    public static void main(String[] args)\n    {\n        String s = "([{}])";\n \n        // Function call\n        if (wellFormed(s))\n            System.out.println("Balanced ");\n        else\n            System.out.println("Not Balanced ");\n    }\n
